<div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 bJMeLZ js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><p align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152991504-005a1daa-2900-4f48-8bec-d163d6336ed2.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152991504-005a1daa-2900-4f48-8bec-d163d6336ed2.png" width="400" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</p>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">欢迎来到 OpenWeedLocator (OWL) 项目，这是一个开源硬件和软件杂草检测器，完全使用现成的组件、非常简单的绿色检测算法（能够升级到作物内检测）和 3D 打印部件。 OWL 将 Raspberry Pi 上的杂草检测与继电器控制板集成在定制设计的外壳中，因此您可以连接任何 12V 电磁阀、继电器、灯泡或设备，以实现低成本、简单且开源的针对特定地点的杂草控制。迄今为止的项目已将 OWL 安装在机器人、车辆和自行车上进行点喷洒。有关最新的想法和新闻，请查看</font></font><a href="https://github.com/geezacoleman/OpenWeedLocator/discussions"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">“讨论”</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">选项卡。</font></font></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">内部电子设备</font></font></th>
<th align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">装配模块 - 车辆</font></font></th>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-official-publications" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#official-publications"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">官方刊物</font></font></h3>
<h4 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-openweedlocator-owl-an-open-source-low-cost-device-for-fallow-weed-detection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#openweedlocator-owl-an-open-source-low-cost-device-for-fallow-weed-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OpenWeedLocator (OWL)：一种用于休耕杂草检测的开源、低成本设备</font></font></h4>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">这是 OWL 的原始出版物，在</font></font><a href="https://www.nature.com/articles/s41598-021-03858-9" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">《科学报告》（开放获取）</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">中发布。测试了一系列绿色检测算法，包括 ExG（过量绿色 2g - r - b，由 Woebecke 等人于 1995 年开发）、色调、饱和度和明度 (HSV) 阈值以及 ExG + HSV 组合算法。如果您在研究中使用 OWL，请考虑引用本出版物。</font></font></p>
<h4 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-investigating-image-based-fallow-weed-detection-performance-on-raphanus-sativus-and-avena-sativa-at-speeds-up-to-30-kmh" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#investigating-image-based-fallow-weed-detection-performance-on-raphanus-sativus-and-avena-sativa-at-speeds-up-to-30-kmh"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">研究以高达 30 km/h 的速度对 Raphanus sativus 和 Avena sativa 基于图像的休耕杂草检测性能</font></font></h4>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OWL 在 5 - 30 公里/小时的速度下使用不同的摄像头在阔叶和禾本科“杂草”上的性能经过测试并发表在</font></font><a href="https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S0168169923008074" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">《农业计算机和电子学》</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">上。目前的 Raspberry Pi HQ Camera + 最新软件组合在 5 公里/小时时提供了 74.8% 的召回率，在 30 公里/小时时提供了 50.5% 的召回率。全局快门 Arducam AR0234 在 5 公里/小时的速度下实现了高达 95.7% 的召回率。</font></font></p>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">存储库 DOI：</font></font><a href="https://zenodo.org/badge/latestdoi/399194159" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6aecb62f19284bd1564af1ba33c467372327b0a22b68e1c1abacf40294f16d22/68747470733a2f2f7a656e6f646f2e6f72672f62616467652f3339393139343135392e737667" alt="DOI" data-canonical-src="https://zenodo.org/badge/399194159.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-raspian-operating-system-support" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#raspian-operating-system-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">Raspian 操作系统支持</font></font></h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">重要提示</font></font></strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">：当前软件只能在 Raspian Buster（支持 picamera）上正常运行。我们正在努力更新图像，以便与 Raspian Bookworm 一起正常运行，以支持 Raspberry Pi 5 和 Picamera2。预计将于 2024 年 2 月发布。同时，我们建议下载现有映像并使用</font></font><code>update_owl.sh</code><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">.</font></font></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">概述</font></font></h1>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-manuals" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#manuals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">手册</font></font></h3>

<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-owl-use-cases" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#owl-use-cases"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">猫头鹰用例</font></font></h1>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-vehicle-mounted-spot-spraying" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#vehicle-mounted-spot-spraying"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">车载点喷涂</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OWL 的第一个也是最明确的用例是在休耕地特定地点施用除草剂。作为该装置开发和测试的一部分，OWL 团队设计并组装了一个 2 m 点喷喷杆，使用两个 OWL 分别控制四个 12 V 电磁阀。喷杆安装在一辆小型货车/多用途车的后部，喷雾罐位于托盘中，由 12V 汽车电池供电。当每个螺线管被激活以进行演示和测试时，每个喷嘴的指示灯用于更清晰地突出显示。</font></font></p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152991630-fe343f37-5a45-43b0-900c-bb3cad4f1b80.JPG"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152991630-fe343f37-5a45-43b0-900c-bb3cad4f1b80.JPG" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</p>

<tr>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">安装间隙</font></font></td>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">0厘米</font></font></td>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">与喷嘴直接安装在同一杆上，仅高 32 厘米。</font></font></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">前进速度</font></font></td>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">6 - 8 公里/小时</font></font></td>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">图像模糊/激活时间限制前进速度。将 OWL 装置向前推进将快速改善行驶速度和大型绿色杂草。</font></font></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">电磁阀</font></font></td>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-robot-mounted-spot-spraying" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#robot-mounted-spot-spraying"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">机器人安装点喷涂</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">第二个系统与第一个系统相同，是为悉尼大学的 Digifarm 机器人 Agerris Digital Farm Hand 开发的。该系统经常用于试验地区特定地点的杂草控制。它由机器人上的 24V 系统供电，使用 24 - 12V DC/DC 转换器。</font></font></p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152990627-0f89bf92-87bc-4808-a748-33f0742068e4.jpg"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/152990627-0f89bf92-87bc-4808-a748-33f0742068e4.jpg" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-image-data-collection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#image-data-collection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">图像数据采集</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">2022 年 7 月 14 日添加了更新的图像采样方法，允许以设定频率保存整个图像、裁剪到边界框和方形图像。这意味着 OWL 现在可以比以前更轻松地用于图像数据收集。下面提供了每种方法的示例图像。</font></font></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">方法</font></font></strong></th>
<th><strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">代码</font></font></strong></th>
<th><strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">例子</font></font></strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">整体形象</font></font></td>
<td><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">'所有的'</font></font></td>
<td><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178902742-45952737-ee3e-4a36-b9b3-216a19e78eb7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178902742-45952737-ee3e-4a36-b9b3-216a19e78eb7.png" alt="20220714-145951__frame_420" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>
</tr>

<td><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">'bbox'</font></font></td>
<td><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178902795-96bb8068-cf58-4f5a-8819-8ca538add384.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178902795-96bb8068-cf58-4f5a-8819-8ca538add384.png" alt="20220714-145757__frame_420_n_4" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>
</tr>

<td><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">将杂草中心裁剪成正方形</font></font></td>
<td><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">'正方形'</font></font></td>
<td><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178903171-af7f8f1b-9caf-435e-96d0-4f01e76c53fb.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51358498/178903171-af7f8f1b-9caf-435e-96d0-4f01e76c53fb.png" alt="20220714-150328__frame_420_n_4" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-community-development-and-contribution" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#community-development-and-contribution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">社区发展与贡献</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">随着越来越多的 OWL 的建立和休耕杂草控制系统的开发，我们很乐意在这里分享最终结果。请联系我们，我们可以在此页面上传成品系统的图像。</font></font></p>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OWL 现在也有一个</font></font><a href="https://github.com/geezacoleman/OpenWeedLocator/discussions"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">讨论</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">页面。使用此来表达任何想法、建议、评论、已完成的单元或您想提出的其他观点。如果有错误或改进，请提出问题。</font></font></p>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">请查看</font></font><a href="/geezacoleman/OpenWeedLocator/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">贡献页面，</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">了解有关如何贡献和遵循社区准则的所有详细信息。</font></font></p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-hardware-requirements" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#hardware-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">硬件要求</font></font></h1>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">下面提供了完整的组件列表。有关 3D 模型和硬件组装的更多详细信息将在后续部分中提供。以下各项的数量适用于一台 OWL 检测装置。</font></font></p>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-hardware-assembly" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#hardware-assembly"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">硬件组装</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">上面列出的所有组件都是相对“即插即用”的，只需最少的焊接或复杂的电子设备。请仔细遵循这些说明，并在打开电源之前三次检查您的连接，以避免损失</font></font><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magic_smoke" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">魔法烟雾</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">和可能的数百美元。当检测单元连接到 12V 时，切勿更改检测单元上的接线，并始终保持在任何组件的安全工作电压范围内。</font></font></p>
<details>
<summary><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">硬件组装完整指南</font></font></summary>
<br><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">
在开始之前，请查看下面的完整接线图，了解所有内容如何组合在一起。 LED、保险丝和 Bulgin 连接器均安装在 OWL 装置的背面，而不是图中的位置。如果您不想使用或无法使用 Bulgin 连接器，可以使用单独的 3D 模型设计来替代电缆密封套。
</font></font><h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-required-tools" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#required-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Required tools</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Wire strippers</li>
<li>Wire cutters</li>
<li>Soldering iron/solder</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/40649348/156698009-a58ed01b-258f-462a-9524-ba3f8d7ec246.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/40649348/156698009-a58ed01b-258f-462a-9524-ba3f8d7ec246.png" alt="wiring diagram-01" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-1---enclosure-and-mounts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-1---enclosure-and-mounts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 1 - enclosure and mounts</h3>
<p dir="auto">Assembling the components for an OWL unit requires the enclosure and mounts as a minimum. These can be 3D printed on your own printer or printed and delivered from one of the many online stores that offer a 3D printing service. Alternatively, you could create your own enclosure using a plastic electrical box and cutting holes in it, if that's easier. We'll be assuming you have printed out the enclosure and associated parts for the rest of the guide, but please share your finished designs however they turn out!</p>
<p dir="auto">The first few steps don't require the enclosure so you can make a start right away, but while you're working on getting that assembled, make sure you have the pieces printing, they'll be used from Step 4. For a complete device, you'll need: 1 x base, 1 x cover, 1 x RPi mount, 1 x relay mount, 1 x regulator mount, 1 x camera mount and 1 x plug.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-2---soldering" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-2---soldering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 2 - soldering</h3>
<p dir="auto">There are only a few components that need soldering, including the fuse and voltage regulator:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Soldering of voltage regulator pins</li>
<li>Soldering of 12V input wires to voltage regulator pins</li>
<li>Soldering of 5V output wires to voltage regulator pins (micro USB cable)</li>
<li>Soldering of red wire to both fuse terminals</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Carefully check which pins on the voltage regulator correspond to 12V in, GND in, 5V out and GND out prior to soldering.</p>
<p dir="auto">To solder the Micro USB cable to the voltage regulator output, you'll need to cut off the USB A end so you are left with approximately 10cm of cable. Using the wire strippers or a sharp box cutter/knife, remove the rubber sheath around the wires. If you have a data + charging cable you should see red, green, white and black wires. The charging only cables will likely only have the red and black wires. Isolate the red (+5V) and black (GND) wires and strip approximately 5mm off the end. Solder the red wire to the positive output on the voltage regulator and black wire to the GND pin. Once you have finished, it should look like the first panel in the figure below.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong>: Soldering can burn you and generates potentially hazardous smoke! Use appropriate care, fume extractors and PPE to avoid any injury. If you're new to soldering, read through <a href="https://www.makerspaces.com/how-to-solder/" rel="nofollow">this guide</a>, which explains in more detail how to perfect your skills and solder safely.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong>: When soldering, it's best to cover the exposed terminals with glue lined heat shrink to reduce the risk of electrical short circuits.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">Voltage regulator</th>
<th align="center">Voltage regulator pins</th>
<th align="center">Fuse</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/cfbc54497f9b9dcb69a25f9a1eec24f1611cda0474a514b8c943efe65d0b5ea5/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f31326335333230302d636539652d313165622d383132622d353263353161306336323633"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/cfbc54497f9b9dcb69a25f9a1eec24f1611cda0474a514b8c943efe65d0b5ea5/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f31326335333230302d636539652d313165622d383132622d353263353161306336323633" alt="Vreg" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/5402/files/12c53200-ce9e-11eb-812b-52c51a0c6263" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>
<td align="center"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fe0264ea04f0acd051e737687f088e720785ea75f0ac0ad9119794e9d51e9156/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f38356162653538302d643032332d313165622d383765652d633363616434323430366665"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fe0264ea04f0acd051e737687f088e720785ea75f0ac0ad9119794e9d51e9156/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f38356162653538302d643032332d313165622d383765652d633363616434323430366665" alt="Vregpins" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/5402/files/85abe580-d023-11eb-87ee-c3cad42406fe" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>
<td align="center"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/dfadbfeba4c1c0218baa6b424983070ecfaf2f071a8eca13799c83dfc1902f2a/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f32343065336538302d636539652d313165622d386330662d323565323936373230303732"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/dfadbfeba4c1c0218baa6b424983070ecfaf2f071a8eca13799c83dfc1902f2a/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f32343065336538302d636539652d313165622d386330662d323565323936373230303732" alt="Fuse" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/5402/files/240e3e80-ce9e-11eb-8c0f-25e296720072" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">Once the two red wires are soldered to the fuse, the fuse can be mounted on the rear panel of the OWL base. One wire will be connected to the Bulgin plug (next step) and the other to the Wago 2-way block.</p>
<p dir="auto">For neater wiring you can also solder jumpers between all the normally open (NO) pins on the base of the relay board, but this is optional. If you don't solder these connections, make sure you connect wire using the screw terminals instead. Photos of both are provided below.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">The other wires requiring soldering are joins between the buzzer and jumper wires for easy connection to the GPIO pins and from the LEDs to the power in/jumper wires.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-3---wiring-up-bulgin-connector" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-3---wiring-up-bulgin-connector"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 3 - wiring up Bulgin connector</h3>
<p dir="auto">Next we'll need to wire the output relay control and input 12V wires to the Bulgin panel mount connector. Fortunately all pins are labelled, so follow the wire number table below. This will need to be repeated for the Bulgin plug as well, which will connect your solenoids or other devices to the relay control board.</p>
<p dir="auto">The process is:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Connect all wires to Bulgin connector using the screw terminals</li>
<li>Mount the connector to the rear panel</li>
<li>Leave at least 10cm of wire so it can be connected to the relay board and other connections later.</li>
</ol>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">Bulgin terminal number</th>
<th align="center">Wire connection</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">1</td>
<td align="center">Blue wire - connects to centre terminal (common) on relay 1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">2</td>
<td align="center">Green wire - connects to centre terminal (common) on relay 2</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">3</td>
<td align="center">Orange wire - connects to centre terminal (common) on relay 3</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">4</td>
<td align="center">White wire - connects to centre terminal (common) on relay 4</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">5</td>
<td align="center">Red 12VDC - connects to fuse wire already soldered. Make sure wire is the right length when mounted.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">6</td>
<td align="center">Black GND - connects to Wago 2-way terminal</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong>: Skip this step if you're using cable glands.</p>
<p dir="auto">Once all the wires have been connected you can now mount the Bulgin connector to the OWL base.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-4---mounting-the-relay-control-board-and-voltage-regulator" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-4---mounting-the-relay-control-board-and-voltage-regulator"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 4 - mounting the relay control board and voltage regulator</h3>
<p dir="auto">Attach the relay control board to the 3D printed relay control board mount using 2.5 mm standoffs. Attach the voltage regulator to the 3D printed voltage regulator mount with 2 mm standoffs. The mounted voltage regulator can then be mounted to one corner of the relay control board. The relay board and voltage regulator can then be installed in the raised slots in the OWL base.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong>: Use <strong>2.5 mm</strong> standoffs for mounting the relay control board to its base. Use <strong>2 mm</strong> standoffs to mount the voltage regulator to its base.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e7ac26337c674bb73b4b39c8d30c95daecc989471b488eb4c73b293f4640c16a/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f39363463353530302d636636612d313165622d386432662d653132383262363431316333"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e7ac26337c674bb73b4b39c8d30c95daecc989471b488eb4c73b293f4640c16a/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f39363463353530302d636636612d313165622d386432662d653132383262363431316333" alt="Relaymount" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/5402/files/964c5500-cf6a-11eb-8d2f-e1282b6411c3" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-5---wiring-the-relay-control-board-voltage-regulator-wago-2-way-blocks-and-bulgin-connector" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-5---wiring-the-relay-control-board-voltage-regulator-wago-2-way-blocks-and-bulgin-connector"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 5 - wiring the relay control board, voltage regulator, Wago 2-way blocks and Bulgin connector</h3>
<p dir="auto">Connect the relay control board to the Bulgin connector using the table in step 3 as a guide.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong>: Some relay control boards such as <a href="https://www.amazon.com/ELEGOO-Channel-Optocoupler-Arduino-Raspberry/dp/B01HEQF5HU/ref=asc_df_B01HEQF5HU/?tag=hyprod-20&amp;linkCode=df0&amp;hvadid=198076677096&amp;hvpos=&amp;hvnetw=g&amp;hvrand=5997956897740931812&amp;hvpone=&amp;hvptwo=&amp;hvqmt=&amp;hvdev=c&amp;hvdvcmdl=&amp;hvlocint=&amp;hvlocphy=9027902&amp;hvtargid=pla-350609711896&amp;psc=1" rel="nofollow">this</a> on Amazon are ACTIVE on LOW. This means that the signal provided by the Raspberry Pi (a higher voltage) to activate a relay will instead turn the relay off. While this can be changed in the code, please consider purchasing HIGH level trigger (e.g <a href="https://www.jaycar.com.au/arduino-compatible-4-channel-12v-relay-module/p/XC4440" rel="nofollow">the board specified in the parts list</a>) or adjustable trigger (e.g. <a href="https://www.amazon.com/DZS-Elec-Optocoupler-Isolation-Triggered/dp/B07BDJJTLZ/ref=asc_df_B07BDJJTLZ/?tag=hyprod-20&amp;linkCode=df0&amp;hvadid=241912880102&amp;hvpos=&amp;hvnetw=g&amp;hvrand=5997956897740931812&amp;hvpone=&amp;hvptwo=&amp;hvqmt=&amp;hvdev=c&amp;hvdvcmdl=&amp;hvlocint=&amp;hvlocphy=9027902&amp;hvtargid=pla-438273746158&amp;psc=1" rel="nofollow">this board</a>).</p>
<p dir="auto">Next, connect red and black jumper wires to the VCC and GND header pins on the relay control board. Now choose one Wago block to be a 12V positive block and the second to be the negative or ground. To the positive block, connect the 12 V wire from the fuse (12V input from source), the 12 V input to the voltage regulator, the 12 V solenoid line from the relay board and the VCC line from the relay board to one of the two WAGO terminal blocks, twisting the wires together if necessary. Repeat with the second, negative WAGO terminal block, connecting the input ground line from the Bulgin connector, ground line from the voltage regulator and the GND black wire from the relay board.</p>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-6---mounting-raspberry-pi-and-connecting-power" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-6---mounting-raspberry-pi-and-connecting-power"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 6 - mounting Raspberry Pi and connecting power</h3>
<p dir="auto">Attach the Raspberry Pi to the 3D printed mount using 2.5 mm standoffs. Install in the raised slots in the OWL base. Connect to micro USB power from the voltage regulator, using a micro USB to USB-C adaptor. Alternatively, the Raspberry Pi can be powered over the GPIO, however, this has not yet been implemented.</p>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-7---connecting-gpio-pins" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-7---connecting-gpio-pins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 7 - connecting GPIO pins</h3>
<p dir="auto">Connect the Raspberry Pi GPIO to the relay control board header pins, using the table below and the wiring diagram above as a guide:</p>
<p dir="auto">The GPIO pins on the Raspberry Pi are not clearly labelled, so use this guide to help. Be careful when connecting these pins as incorrect wiring can shortcircuit/damage your Pi.

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-8---mounting-and-connecting-camera" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-8---mounting-and-connecting-camera"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 8 - mounting and connecting camera</h3>
<p dir="auto">Connect one end of the CSI ribbon cable to the camera. We provide a mounting plate that can be used with both the HQ or V2 cameras, however, we recommend the use of the HQ camera for improved image clarity. Attach the HQ camera to the 3D printed mount using 2.5 mm standoffs (or 2 mm standoffs if using the V2 camera). Ensuring that the CSI cable port on the camera is directed towards the Raspberry Pi, mount the camera inside the OWL case using four M3 standoffs (50 mm long for HQ camera; 20 mm long for V2 camera). Connect the other end of the CSI cable to the Raspberry Pi CSI camera port.</p>
<p dir="auto">Before connecting the lens, please be aware the HQ camera comes with fitted a C-CS mount adapter which needs to be removed before fitting the 6mm lens. The image won't focus unless the adapter is removed. More information is available below and in the <a href="https://datasheets.raspberrypi.com/hq-camera/cs-mount-lens-guide.pdf" rel="nofollow">HQ Camera Datasheet</a></p>
<p dir="auto">How to remove the C-CS mount adapter:</p>

<p dir="auto">The HQ lens will need to be focused, details below, once the software is correctly set up.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-9---adding-buzzer-and-leds" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-9---adding-buzzer-and-leds"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 9 - adding buzzer and LEDs</h3>
<p dir="auto">Mount the buzzer inside the OWL base using double sided mounting tape and connect the 5 V and ground wires to Raspberry Pi GPIO pins 7 and 9, respectively.</p>
<p dir="auto">For simplicity we have used two 12V LEDs (which are just normal LEDs with a current limiting resistor included) for both the 5V TX/GND connection for Raspberry Pi status indication and also the 12V power connection. While 12 V will work fine on both, the 5 V connection will be dimmer. If you want to use a non-prepackaged, 3 mm LED for the 5V connection, you should solder a current limiting resistor to the LED to prevent damage to either the LED or the Rasperry Pi as described <a href="https://howchoo.com/g/ytzjyzy4m2e/build-a-simple-raspberry-pi-led-power-status-indicator" rel="nofollow">here</a>. Install the 5 V LED inside the OWL base and connect the 5V and ground wire to GPIO pins 8 (TX pin) and 20 (GND pin), respectively. Install the 12 V LED inside the OWL base and connect the 12 V and GND wires to their respective WAGO terminal blocks.</p>

<td align="center"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2d07f5d57c70a5c9d13521df3ab3a10926b833f9ccaf08e1714fd0f1eb2a9d47/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f65303437343038302d643032372d313165622d393366642d386337623763373833656561"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2d07f5d57c70a5c9d13521df3ab3a10926b833f9ccaf08e1714fd0f1eb2a9d47/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f353430322f66696c65732f65303437343038302d643032372d313165622d393366642d386337623763373833656561" alt="GPIOpins" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/5402/files/e0474080-d027-11eb-93fd-8c7b7c783eea" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></td>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-optional-step---adding-real-time-clock-module" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#optional-step---adding-real-time-clock-module"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>OPTIONAL STEP - adding real time clock module</h3>
<p dir="auto">Although optional, we recommend that you use a real time clock (RTC) module with the OWL system. This will enable the Raspberry Pi to hold the correct time when disconnected from power and the internet, and will be useful for debugging errors if they arise. The RTC uses a CR1220 button cell battery and sits on top of the Raspberry Pi using GPIO pins 1-6.</p>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-10---connecting-mounting-hardware-and-owl-cover" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-10---connecting-mounting-hardware-and-owl-cover"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 10 - connecting mounting hardware and OWL cover</h3>
<p dir="auto">There are four 6.5 mm holes on the OWL base for mounting to a boom. Prior to installing the OWL cover, decide on a mounting solution suitable to your needs. In the photo below, we used 4 x M6 bolts. The cover of the OWL unit is secured with 4 x M3 nuts and bolts. Place M3 nuts into the slots in the OWL base. This can be fiddly and we suggest using tweezers, as shown below. Place the cover onto the base and secure using M3 bolts.</p>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-11---connecting-12v-solenoids" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-11---connecting-12v-solenoids"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 11 - connecting 12V solenoids</h3>
<p dir="auto">Once you have completed the setup, you now have the opportunity to wire up your own solenoids for spot spraying, targeted tillage, spot flaming or any other targeted weed control you can dream up. To do this, wire the GND wire of your device (it can be any wire if it's a solenoid) to the ground pin on the Bulgin plug (the same wire used for the GND from the 12V power source) and wire the other to one of the blue, green, orange or white wires on pins 1 - 4. A wiring diagram is provided below. The easiest way to wire them together to the same GND wire is to create a six-way harness, where one end is connected to the plug, one of the five other wires to the source power GND and the remaining four to the solenoids or whatever devices you are driving.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/40649348/156698481-3d4fec4e-567a-4a18-b72e-b26d35c8d1c7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/40649348/156698481-3d4fec4e-567a-4a18-b72e-b26d35c8d1c7.png" alt="solenoid wiring-01" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-sbc-options" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#sbc-options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">SBC 选项</font></font></h3>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">单板计算机或 SBC 是 OWL 背后的大脑。它可以在一块信用卡大小的板上完成所有图像处理和逻辑，无需移动部件。这些 SBC 是嵌入式计算或“边缘计算”的支柱。虽然 Raspberry Pi 可以说是使用最广泛且支持良好的 SBC 之一，但仍有许多不同的选择。每个人都有自己的优点和缺点，可能适合也可能不适合 OWL。我们在下面提供了一些 SBC 的摘要，但这并不是详尽的列表。</font></font></p>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">目前，只有 Raspberry Pi 4 和 3B+ 可与 OWL 配合使用，并且已经过全面测试。早期测试（alpha）是使用 LibreComputer LePotato 进行的。随着更多的主板在社区中进行测试，我们将更新“与 OWL 配合使用”专栏。</font></font></p>

<h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-software" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#software"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">软件</font></font></h1>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">该项目最终将支持使用两种主要的嵌入式计算设备：Raspberry Pi（型号 3B+ 和 4）和 Jetson Nano/Jetson Xavier NX，通过深度学习算法实现可能的绿色对绿色检测。目前，下面仅提供设置 Raspberry Pi 3B+/4 的详细信息。有两种安装选项。首先，您需要做的就是下载磁盘映像文件 (vX.XX-owl.img) 并将其闪存到 SD 卡。第二种方法更深入，但会带您从头到尾完成整个过程。如果您想了解一切是如何运作的，请花一些时间完成此过程。</font></font></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">注意：</font></font></strong><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">在 2023 年 3 月 17 日的主要更新中，OWL 的运行从使用更改</font></font><code>greenonbrown.py</code><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">为</font></font><code>owl.py</code><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">.这确保了与 GoG 算法更好的交叉兼容性。它提高了系统的模块化程度。</font></font></p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-quick-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#quick-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">快速方法</font></font></h2>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">对于此方法，您需要访问：</font></font></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">台式/笔记本电脑</font></font></li>
<li><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">微型 SD 读卡器</font></font></li>
<li><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">数据容量大、速度快的互联网（警告：图像文件很大，如果您的套餐有限，下载将花费时间并耗尽您的大量数据流量）</font></font></li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary><b><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">软件快速安装方法</font></font></b></summary>
<br>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-1---download-the-disk-image-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-1---download-the-disk-image-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 1 - download the disk image file</h3>
<p dir="auto">Download the entire disk image file (v1.0.0-owl.img) here: <a href="https://www.dropbox.com/s/ad6uieyk3awav9k/owl.img.zip?dl=0" rel="nofollow">OWL disk image</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE</strong> The v1.0.0-owl.img file contains the original software and we strongly recommend updating using the process below. It also includes the deprecated naming of <code>greenonbrown.py</code> instead of <code>owl.py</code>. If you do not update the software, be aware that you will need to run <code>greenonbrown.py</code> instead.</p>
<p dir="auto">The latest, stable version will be linked above, however, all other older versions or versions with features being tested are available <a href="#version-history">here</a>.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-2---flash-owlimg-to-sd-card" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-2---flash-owlimg-to-sd-card"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 2 - flash owl.img to SD card</h3>
<p dir="auto">The easiest way to flash (add the vX.X.X-owl.img file to the SD card so it can boot) the SD card is to use Balena Etcher or any other card flashing software. Instructions for Balena Etcher are provided here. Navigate to the <a href="https://www.balena.io/etcher/" rel="nofollow">website</a> and download the relevant version/operating system. Install Balena Etcher and fire it up.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ea6334dfa7ad481a4b07b3516afc9af5a2b8900f6e428cc0c60d7711f2fe19f8/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f333835392f66696c65732f65313834656130302d643561302d313165622d393536302d343834323735383638366430"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ea6334dfa7ad481a4b07b3516afc9af5a2b8900f6e428cc0c60d7711f2fe19f8/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6769746875622e7379646e65792e6564752e61752f757365722f333835392f66696c65732f65313834656130302d643561302d313165622d393536302d343834323735383638366430" alt="OWL - etcher" data-canonical-src="https://media.github.sydney.edu.au/user/3859/files/e184ea00-d5a0-11eb-9560-4842758686d0" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Insert the SD card using your SD card reader.</li>
<li>Select <code>Flash from file</code> on the Balena Etcher window and navigate to where you downloaded the vXX-XX-XX-owl.dmg file. This can be a zip file (compressed) too.</li>
<li>Select the target, the SD card you just inserted.</li>
<li>Click <code>Flash</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If this completes successfully, you're ready to move to the next step. If it fails, use Balena Etcher documentation to diagnose the issue.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-3---power-up" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-3---power-up"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 3 - power up</h3>
<p dir="auto">Once the SD card is inserted into the slot of the Raspberry Pi, power everything up and wait for the beep. If you hear the beep, you're ready to go and start focusing the camera.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-4---updating-the-disk-image" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-4---updating-the-disk-image"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 4 - updating the disk image</h3>
<p dir="auto">The disk image that you downloaded is likely to be a few versions behind the most recent. We only provide images of the most major updates. So to update the OWL software, just run the follow these steps.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Have the OWL powered on with screen, keyboard and mouse connected. You should see a desktop with the OWL logo.</li>
<li>Press CTRL + ALT + T to open a Terminal window or click the black icon with blue line and &gt;_ symbol.</li>
<li>Once the Terminal window is open, make sure you are working in the <code>owl</code> virtual environment by running:</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>pi@raspberrypi:~ $ workon owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $
</code></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 tooltipped-no-delay d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="pi@raspberrypi:~ $ workon owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">Notice that (owl) now appears before the line in the Terminal window. This indicates you are in the <code>owl</code> virtual environment. This is <strong>critical</strong> to make sure you install everything in the <code>requirements.txt</code> file into the right spot.</p>
<ol start="4" dir="auto">
<li>Once you are in the <code>owl</code> environment, enter these commands on each new line:</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ mv owl owl-old      # this renames the old 'owl' folder to 'owl-old'
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ git clone https://github.com/geezacoleman/OpenWeedLocator        # download the new software
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ mv OpenWeedLocator owl      # rename the download to 'owl'
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~/owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ pip install -r requirements.txt                # installs the necessary software into the (owl) environment 
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ chmod a+x owl.py                  # changes owl.py to be executable
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ chmod a+x owl_boot.sh                     # changes owl_boot.sh to be executable
</code></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 tooltipped-no-delay d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ mv owl owl-old      # this renames the old 'owl' folder to 'owl-old'
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ git clone https://github.com/geezacoleman/OpenWeedLocator        # download the new software
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ mv OpenWeedLocator owl      # rename the download to 'owl'
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~/owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ pip install -r requirements.txt                # installs the necessary software into the (owl) environment 
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ chmod a+x owl.py                  # changes owl.py to be executable
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ chmod a+x owl_boot.sh                     # changes owl_boot.sh to be executable" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">Once this is complete your software will be up to date and you can move on to focusing the camera.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-step-5---focusing-the-camera" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#step-5---focusing-the-camera"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Step 5 - focusing the camera</h3>
<p dir="auto">The final step in the process is to make sure the camera is correctly focused for the mounting height. With the latest software, when you run <code>owl.py --focus</code> a sharpness (i.e. least blurry) estimation is provided on the video feed. The algorithm determines how sharp an image is, so the higher the value the better. A single script is provided to make focusing as easy as possible. Simply run:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~/owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ bash focus_owl.sh 
</code></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 tooltipped-no-delay d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~ $ cd ~/owl
(owl) pi@raspberrypi:~/owl $ bash focus_owl.sh " tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<p dir="auto">This will automate all the steps below. If this doesn't work, follow the steps below. If you would like to focus the OWL again, you can always run <code>./owl.py --focus</code>.</p>
